    29	import { computeUtilitySignature } from './signatures'
    30	
    31	export type Migration = (
    32	  designSystem: DesignSystem,
    33	  userConfig: Config | null,
    34	  rawCandidate: string,
    35	) => string | Promise<string>
    36	
    37	export const DEFAULT_MIGRATIONS: Migration[] = [
    38	  migrateEmptyArbitraryValues,
    39	  migratePrefix,
    40	  migrateCanonicalizeCandidate,
    41	  migrateBgGradient,
    42	  migrateSimpleLegacyClasses,
    43	  migrateCamelcaseInNamedValue,
    44	  migrateLegacyClasses,
    45	  migrateMaxWidthScreen,
    46	  migrateThemeToVar,
    47	  migrateVariantOrder, // Has to happen before migrations that modify variants
    48	  migrateAutomaticVarInjection,
    49	  migrateLegacyArbitraryValues,
    50	  migrateArbitraryUtilities,
    51	  migrateBareValueUtilities,
    52	  migrateDeprecatedUtilities,
    53	  migrateModernizeArbitraryValues,
    54	  migrateArbitraryVariants,
    55	  migrateDropUnnecessaryDataTypes,
    56	  migrateArbitraryValueToBareValue,
    57	  migrateOptimizeModifier,
    58	]
    59	
    60	let migrateCached = new DefaultMap<
    61	  DesignSystem,
    62	  DefaultMap<Config | null, DefaultMap<string, Promise<string>>>
    63	>((designSystem) => {
    64	  return new DefaultMap((userConfig) => {
    65	    return new DefaultMap(async (rawCandidate) => {
    66	      let original = rawCandidate
    67	
    68	      for (let migration of DEFAULT_MIGRATIONS) {
    69	        rawCandidate = await migration(designSystem, userConfig, rawCandidate)
    70	      }
    71	
    72	      // Verify that the candidate actually makes sense at all. E.g.: `duration`
    73	      // is not a valid candidate, but it will parse because `duration-<number>`
    74	      // exists.
    75	      let signature = computeUtilitySignature.get(designSystem).get(rawCandidate)
    76	      if (typeof signature !== 'string') return original
    77	
    78	      return rawCandidate
    79	    })
    80	  })
    81	})
    82	
    83	export async function migrateCandidate(
    84	  designSystem: DesignSystem,
    85	  userConfig: Config | null,
    86	  rawCandidate: string,
    87	  // Location is only set when migrating a candidate from a source file
    88	  location?: {
    89	    contents: string
    90	    start: number
    91	    end: number
    92	  },
    93	): Promise<string> {
    94	  // Skip this migration if we think that the migration is unsafe
    95	  if (location && !isSafeMigration(rawCandidate, location, designSystem)) {
    96	    return rawCandidate
    97	  }
    98	
    99	  return migrateCached.get(designSystem).get(userConfig).get(rawCandidate)
   100	}
   101	
   102	export default async function migrateContents(
   103	  designSystem: DesignSystem,
   104	  userConfig: Config | null,
   105	  contents: string,
   106	  extension: string,
   107	): Promise<string> {
   108	  let candidates = await extractRawCandidates(contents, extension)
   109	
   110	  let changes: StringChange[] = []
   111	
   112	  for (let { rawCandidate, start, end } of candidates) {
   113	    let migratedCandidate = await migrateCandidate(designSystem, userConfig, rawCandidate, {
   114	      contents,
   115	      start,
   116	      end,
   117	    })
   118	
   119	    if (migratedCandidate === rawCandidate) {
   120	      continue
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    changes.push({
   124	      start,
   125	      end,
   126	      replacement: migratedCandidate,
   127	    })
   128	  }
   129	
   130	  return spliceChangesIntoString(contents, changes)
   131	}
   132	
   133	export async function migrate(designSystem: DesignSystem, userConfig: Config | null, file: string) {
   134	  let fullPath = path.isAbsolute(file) ? file : path.resolve(process.cwd(), file)
   135	  let contents = await fs.readFile(fullPath, 'utf-8')
   136	
   137	  await fs.writeFile(
   138	    fullPath,
   139	    await migrateContents(designSystem, userConfig, contents, extname(file)),
   140	  )
   141	}
   142

str_replace_editor view /testbed/packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/is-safe-migration.ts
2025-12-26 09:35:47,535 - DEBUG - swea-tools - Retrieved state from environment: {'working_dir': '/testbed'}
2025-12-26 09:35:47,539 - INFO - swea-agent - 🤖 MODEL INPUT

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/is-safe-migration.ts:
     1	import { parseCandidate } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/candidate'
     2	import type { DesignSystem } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/design-system'
     3	import { DefaultMap } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/utils/default-map'
     4	import * as version from '../../utils/version'
     5	
     6	const QUOTES = ['"', "'", '`']
     7	const LOGICAL_OPERATORS = ['&&', '||', '?', '===', '==', '!=', '!==', '>', '>=', '<', '<=']
     8	const CONDITIONAL_TEMPLATE_SYNTAX = [
     9	  // Vue
    10	  /v-else-if=['"]$/,
    11	  /v-if=['"]$/,
    12	  /v-show=['"]$/,
    13	  /(?<!:?class)=['"]$/,
    14	
    15	  // Alpine
    16	  /x-if=['"]$/,
    17	  /x-show=['"]$/,
    18	  /wire:[^\s]*?$/,
    19	]
    20	const NEXT_PLACEHOLDER_PROP = /placeholder=\{?['"]$/
    21	const VUE_3_EMIT = /\b\$?emit\(['"]$/
    22	
    23	export function isSafeMigration(
    24	  rawCandidate: string,
    25	  location: { contents: string; start: number; end: number },
    26	  designSystem: DesignSystem,
    27	): boolean {
    28	  // Ensure we are not migrating a candidate in a `<style>` block. The heuristic
    29	  // would be if the candidate is preceded by a whitespace and followed by a
    30	  // colon and whitespace.
    31	  //
    32	  // E.g.:
    33	  // ```vue
    34	  // <template>
    35	  //   <div class="foo"></div>
    36	  // </template>
    37	  //
    38	  //
    39	  // <style>
    40	  // .foo {
    41	  //   flex-shrink: 0;
    42	  //  ^           ^^
    43	  // }
    44	  // </style>
    45	  // ```
    46	  if (
    47	    // Whitespace before the candidate
    48	    location.contents[location.start - 1]?.match(/\s/) &&
    49	    // A colon followed by whitespace after the candidate
    50	    location.contents.slice(location.end, location.end + 2)?.match(/^:\s/)
    51	  ) {
    52	    // Compute all `<style>` ranges once and cache it for the current files
    53	    let ranges = styleBlockRanges.get(location.contents)
    54	
    55	    for (let i = 0; i < ranges.length; i += 2) {
    56	      let start = ranges[i]
    57	      let end = ranges[i + 1]
    58	
    59	      // Check if the candidate is inside a `<style>` block
    60	      if (location.start >= start && location.end <= end) {
    61	        return false
    62	      }
    63	    }
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  let [candidate] = parseCandidate(rawCandidate, designSystem)
    67	
    68	  // If we can't parse the candidate, then it's not a candidate at all. However,
    69	  // we could be dealing with legacy classes like `tw__flex` in Tailwind CSS v3
    70	  // land, which also wouldn't parse.
    71	  //
    72	  // So let's only skip if we couldn't parse and we are not in Tailwind CSS v3.
    73	  //
    74	  if (!candidate && version.isGreaterThan(3)) {
    75	    return false
    76	  }
    77	
    78	  // Parsed a candidate successfully, verify if it's a valid candidate
    79	  else if (candidate) {
    80	    // When we have variants, we can assume that the candidate is safe to migrate
    81	    // because that requires colons.
    82	    //
    83	    // E.g.: `hover:focus:flex`
    84	    if (candidate.variants.length > 0) {
    85	      return true
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    // When we have an arbitrary property, the candidate has such a particular
    89	    // structure it's very likely to be safe.
    90	    //
    91	    // E.g.: `[color:red]`
    92	    if (candidate.kind === 'arbitrary') {
    93	      return true
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    // A static candidate is very likely safe if it contains a dash.
    97	    //
    98	    // E.g.: `items-center`
    99	    if (candidate.kind === 'static' && candidate.root.includes('-')) {
   100	      return true
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    // A functional candidate is very likely safe if it contains a value (which
   104	    // implies a `-`). Or if the root contains a dash.
   105	    //
   106	    // E.g.: `bg-red-500`, `bg-position-20`
   107	    if (
   108	      (candidate.kind === 'functional' && candidate.value !== null) ||
   109	      (candidate.kind === 'functional' && candidate.root.includes('-'))
   110	    ) {
   111	      return true
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    // If the candidate contains a modifier, it's very likely to be safe because
   115	    // it implies that it contains a `/`.
   116	    //
   117	    // E.g.: `text-sm/7`
   118	    if (candidate.kind === 'functional' && candidate.modifier) {
   119	      return true
   120	    }
   121	  }
   122	
   123	  let currentLineBeforeCandidate = ''
   124	  for (let i = location.start - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   125	    let char = location.contents.at(i)!
   126	    if (char === '\n') {
   127	      break
   128	    }
   129	    currentLineBeforeCandidate = char + currentLineBeforeCandidate
   130	  }
   131	  let currentLineAfterCandidate = ''
   132	  for (let i = location.end; i < location.contents.length; i++) {
   133	    let char = location.contents.at(i)!
   134	    if (char === '\n') {
   135	      break
   136	    }
   137	    currentLineAfterCandidate += char
   138	  }
   139	
   140	  // Heuristic: Require the candidate to be inside quotes
   141	  let isQuoteBeforeCandidate = QUOTES.some((quote) => currentLineBeforeCandidate.includes(quote))
   142	  let isQuoteAfterCandidate = QUOTES.some((quote) => currentLineAfterCandidate.includes(quote))
   143	  if (!isQuoteBeforeCandidate || !isQuoteAfterCandidate) {
   144	    return false
   145	  }
   146	
   147	  // Heuristic: Disallow object access immediately following the candidate
   148	  if (currentLineAfterCandidate[0] === '.') {
   149	    return false
   150	  }
   151	
   152	  // Heuristic: Disallow function call expressions immediately following the candidate
   153	  if (currentLineAfterCandidate.trim().startsWith('(')) {
   154	    return false
   155	  }
   156	
   157	  // Heuristic: Disallow logical operators preceding or following the candidate
   158	  for (let operator of LOGICAL_OPERATORS) {
   159	    if (
   160	      currentLineAfterCandidate.trim().startsWith(operator) ||
   161	      currentLineBeforeCandidate.trim().endsWith(operator)
   162	    ) {
   163	      return false
   164	    }
   165	  }
   166	
   167	  // Heuristic: Disallow conditional template syntax
   168	  for (let rule of CONDITIONAL_TEMPLATE_SYNTAX) {
   169	    if (rule.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
   170	      return false
   171	    }
   172	  }
   173	
   174	  // Heuristic: Disallow Next.js Image `placeholder` prop
   175	  if (NEXT_PLACEHOLDER_PROP.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
   176	    return false
   177	  }
   178	
   179	  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements inside `emit('…', …)`
   180	  if (VUE_3_EMIT.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
   181	    return false
   182	  }
   183	
   184	  return true
   185	}
   186	
   187	// Assumptions:
   188	// - All `<style` tags appear before the next `</style>` tag
   189	// - All `<style` tags are closed with `</style>`
   190	// - No nested `<style>` tags
   191	const styleBlockRanges = new DefaultMap((source: string) => {
   192	  let ranges: number[] = []
   193	  let offset = 0
   194	
   195	  while (true) {
   196	    let startTag = source.indexOf('<style', offset)
   197	    if (startTag === -1) return ranges
   198	
   199	    offset = startTag + 1
   200	
   201	    // Ensure the style looks like:
   202	    // - `<style>`   (closed)
   203	    // - `<style …>` (with attributes)
   204	    if (!source[startTag + 6].match(/[>\s]/)) continue
   205	
   206	    let endTag = source.indexOf('</style>', offset)
   207	    if (endTag === -1) return ranges
   208	    offset = endTag + 1
   209	
   210	    ranges.push(startTag, endTag)
   211	  }
   212	})
   213

     1	import { Scanner } from '@tailwindcss/oxide'
     2	import type { Candidate } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/candidate'
     3	import type { DesignSystem } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/design-system'
     4	
     5	export async function extractRawCandidates(
     6	  content: string,
     7	  extension: string = 'html',
     8	): Promise<{ rawCandidate: string; start: number; end: number }[]> {
     9	  let scanner = new Scanner({})
    10	  let result = scanner.getCandidatesWithPositions({ content, extension })
    11	
    12	  let candidates: { rawCandidate: string; start: number; end: number }[] = []
    13	  for (let { candidate: rawCandidate, position: start } of result) {
    14	    candidates.push({ rawCandidate, start, end: start + rawCandidate.length })
    15	  }
    16	  return candidates
    17	}
    18	
    19	// Create a basic stripped candidate without variants or important flag
    20	export function baseCandidate<T extends Candidate>(candidate: T) {
    21	  let base = structuredClone(candidate)
    22	
    23	  base.important = false
    24	  base.variants = []
    25	
    26	  return base
    27	}
    28	
    29	export function parseCandidate(designSystem: DesignSystem, input: string) {
    30	  return designSystem.parseCandidate(
    31	    designSystem.theme.prefix && !input.startsWith(`${designSystem.theme.prefix}:`)
    32	      ? `${designSystem.theme.prefix}:${input}`
    33	      : input,
    34	  )
    35	}
    36	
    37	export function printUnprefixedCandidate(designSystem: DesignSystem, candidate: Candidate) {
    38	  let candidateString = designSystem.printCandidate(candidate)
    39	
    40	  return designSystem.theme.prefix && candidateString.startsWith(`${designSystem.theme.prefix}:`)
    41	    ? candidateString.slice(designSystem.theme.prefix.length + 1)
    42	    : candidateString
    43	}
    44

     1	import type { Config } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/compat/plugin-api'
     2	import type { DesignSystem } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/design-system'
     3	import * as version from '../../utils/version'
     4	
     5	// Classes that used to exist in Tailwind CSS v3, but do not exist in Tailwind
     6	// CSS v4 anymore.
     7	const LEGACY_CLASS_MAP: Record<string, string> = {
     8	  'overflow-ellipsis': 'text-ellipsis',
     9	
    10	  'flex-grow': 'grow',
    11	  'flex-grow-0': 'grow-0',
    12	  'flex-shrink': 'shrink',
    13	  'flex-shrink-0': 'shrink-0',
    14	
    15	  'decoration-clone': 'box-decoration-clone',
    16	  'decoration-slice': 'box-decoration-slice',
    17	
    18	  // Since v4.1.0
    19	  'bg-left-top': 'bg-top-left',
    20	  'bg-left-bottom': 'bg-bottom-left',
    21	  'bg-right-top': 'bg-top-right',
    22	  'bg-right-bottom': 'bg-bottom-right',
    23	  'object-left-top': 'object-top-left',
    24	  'object-left-bottom': 'object-bottom-left',
    25	  'object-right-top': 'object-top-right',
    26	  'object-right-bottom': 'object-bottom-right',
    27	}
    28	
    29	let seenDesignSystems = new WeakSet<DesignSystem>()
    30	
    31	export function migrateSimpleLegacyClasses(
    32	  designSystem: DesignSystem,
    33	  _userConfig: Config | null,
    34	  rawCandidate: string,
    35	): string {
    36	  // `outline-none` in v3 has the same meaning as `outline-hidden` in v4. However,
    37	  // `outline-none` in v4 _also_ exists but has a different meaning.
    38	  //
    39	  // We can only migrate `outline-none` to `outline-hidden` if we are migrating a
    40	  // v3 project to v4.
    41	  if (version.isMajor(3)) {
    42	    LEGACY_CLASS_MAP['outline-none'] = 'outline-hidden'
    43	  }
    44	
    45	  // Prepare design system with the unknown legacy classes
    46	  if (!seenDesignSystems.has(designSystem)) {
    47	    for (let old in LEGACY_CLASS_MAP) {
    48	      designSystem.utilities.static(old, () => [])
    49	    }
    50	    seenDesignSystems.add(designSystem)
    51	  }
    52	
    53	  for (let candidate of designSystem.parseCandidate(rawCandidate)) {
    54	    if (candidate.kind === 'static' && Object.hasOwn(LEGACY_CLASS_MAP, candidate.root)) {
    55	      return designSystem.printCandidate({
    56	        ...candidate,
    57	        root: LEGACY_CLASS_MAP[candidate.root as keyof typeof LEGACY_CLASS_MAP],
    58	      })
    59	    }
    60	  }
    61	
    62	  return rawCandidate
    63	}
    64

     1	import { __unstable__loadDesignSystem } from '@tailwindcss/node'
     2	import path from 'node:path'
     3	import url from 'node:url'
     4	import type { Candidate } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/candidate'
     5	import type { Config } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/compat/plugin-api'
     6	import type { DesignSystem } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/design-system'
     7	import { DefaultMap } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/utils/default-map'
     8	import * as version from '../../utils/version'
     9	import { baseCandidate } from './candidates'
    10	
    11	const __filename = url.fileURLToPath(import.meta.url)
    12	const __dirname = path.dirname(__filename)
    13	
    14	const LEGACY_CLASS_MAP = new Map([
    15	  ['shadow', 'shadow-sm'],
    16	  ['shadow-sm', 'shadow-xs'],
    17	  ['shadow-xs', 'shadow-2xs'],
    18	
    19	  ['inset-shadow', 'inset-shadow-sm'],
    20	  ['inset-shadow-sm', 'inset-shadow-xs'],
    21	  ['inset-shadow-xs', 'inset-shadow-2xs'],
    22	
    23	  ['drop-shadow', 'drop-shadow-sm'],
    24	  ['drop-shadow-sm', 'drop-shadow-xs'],
    25	
    26	  ['rounded', 'rounded-sm'],
    27	  ['rounded-sm', 'rounded-xs'],
    28	
    29	  ['blur', 'blur-sm'],
    30	  ['blur-sm', 'blur-xs'],
    31	
    32	  ['backdrop-blur', 'backdrop-blur-sm'],
    33	  ['backdrop-blur-sm', 'backdrop-blur-xs'],
    34	
    35	  ['ring', 'ring-3'],
    36	
    37	  ['outline', 'outline-solid'],
    38	])
    39	
    40	const THEME_KEYS = new Map([
    41	  ['shadow', '--shadow'],
    42	  ['shadow-sm', '--shadow-sm'],
    43	  ['shadow-xs', '--shadow-xs'],
    44	  ['shadow-2xs', '--shadow-2xs'],
    45	
    46	  ['drop-shadow', '--drop-shadow'],
    47	  ['drop-shadow-sm', '--drop-shadow-sm'],
    48	  ['drop-shadow-xs', '--drop-shadow-xs'],
    49	
    50	  ['rounded', '--radius'],
    51	  ['rounded-sm', '--radius-sm'],
    52	  ['rounded-xs', '--radius-xs'],
    53	
    54	  ['blur', '--blur'],
    55	  ['blur-sm', '--blur-sm'],
    56	  ['blur-xs', '--blur-xs'],
    57	
    58	  ['backdrop-blur', '--backdrop-blur'],
    59	  ['backdrop-blur-sm', '--backdrop-blur-sm'],
    60	  ['backdrop-blur-xs', '--backdrop-blur-xs'],
    61	
    62	  ['ring', '--ring-width'],
    63	  ['ring-3', '--ring-width-3'],
    64	])
    65	
    66	const DESIGN_SYSTEMS = new DefaultMap((base) => {
    67	  return __unstable__loadDesignSystem('@import "tailwindcss";', { base })
    68	})
    69	
    70	export async function migrateLegacyClasses(
    71	  designSystem: DesignSystem,
    72	  _userConfig: Config | null,
    73	  rawCandidate: string,
    74	): Promise<string> {
    75	  // These migrations are only safe when migrating from v3 to v4.
    76	  //
    77	  // Migrating from `rounded` to `rounded-sm` once is fine (v3 -> v4). But if we
    78	  // migrate again (v4 -> v4), then `rounded-sm` would be migrated to
    79	  // `rounded-xs` which is incorrect because we already migrated this.
    80	  if (!version.isMajor(3)) {
    81	    return rawCandidate
    82	  }
    83	
    84	  let defaultDesignSystem = await DESIGN_SYSTEMS.get(__dirname)
    85	
    86	  function* migrate(rawCandidate: string) {
    87	    for (let candidate of designSystem.parseCandidate(rawCandidate)) {
    88	      // Create a base candidate string from the candidate.
    89	      // E.g.: `hover:blur!` -> `blur`
    90	      let base = baseCandidate(candidate)
    91	      let baseCandidateString = designSystem.printCandidate(base)
    92	
    93	      // Find the new base candidate string. `blur` -> `blur-sm`
    94	      let newBaseCandidateString = LEGACY_CLASS_MAP.get(baseCandidateString)
    95	      if (!newBaseCandidateString) continue
    96	
    97	      // Parse the new base candidate string into an actual candidate AST.
    98	      let [newBaseCandidate] = designSystem.parseCandidate(newBaseCandidateString)
    99	      if (!newBaseCandidate) continue
   100	
   101	      // Re-apply the variants and important flag from the original candidate.
   102	      // E.g.: `hover:blur!` -> `blur` -> `blur-sm` -> `hover:blur-sm!`
   103	      let newCandidate = structuredClone(newBaseCandidate) as Candidate
   104	      newCandidate.variants = candidate.variants
   105	      newCandidate.important = candidate.important
   106	
   107	      yield [
   108	        newCandidate,
   109	        THEME_KEYS.get(baseCandidateString),
   110	        THEME_KEYS.get(newBaseCandidateString),
   111	      ] as const
   112	    }
   113	  }
   114	
   115	  for (let [toCandidate, fromThemeKey, toThemeKey] of migrate(rawCandidate)) {
   116	    if (fromThemeKey && toThemeKey) {
   117	      // Migrating something that resolves to a value in the theme.
   118	      let customFrom = designSystem.resolveThemeValue(fromThemeKey, true)
   119	      let defaultFrom = defaultDesignSystem.resolveThemeValue(fromThemeKey, true)
   120	      let customTo = designSystem.resolveThemeValue(toThemeKey, true)
   121	      let defaultTo = defaultDesignSystem.resolveThemeValue(toThemeKey)
   122	
   123	      // The new theme value is not defined, which means we can't safely
   124	      // migrate the utility.
   125	      if (customTo === undefined && defaultTo !== undefined) {
   126	        continue
   127	      }
   128	
   129	      // The "from" theme value changed compared to the default theme value.
   130	      if (customFrom !== defaultFrom) {
   131	        continue
   132	      }
   133	
   134	      // The "to" theme value changed compared to the default theme value.
   135	      if (customTo !== defaultTo) {
   136	        continue
   137	      }
   138	    }
   139	
   140	    return designSystem.printCandidate(toCandidate)
   141	  }
   142	
   143	  return rawCandidate
   144	}
   145

    50	    // deprecated
    51	    ['order-[0]', 'order-0'],
    52	    ['order-0', 'order-0'],
    53	
    54	    // Migrate deprecated named values to bare values
    55	    ['order-none', 'order-0'],
    56	
    57	    // `-0` should not be migrated to `0`.
    58	    //
    59	    // This used to be a bug that translate `mt-[0px]` into `-mt-[0px]` because
    60	    // `-mt-[0px]` translates to `margin-top: calc(0px * -1);` and therefore we
    61	    // handle the `0px * -1` case which translates to `0px` not `-0px`.
    62	    //
    63	    // This translation is actually fine, because now, we will prefer the
    64	    // non-negative version first so we can replace `-mt-[0px]` with `mt-[0px]`.
    65	    ['mt-[0px]', 'mt-[0px]'],
    66	    ['-mt-[0px]', 'mt-[0px]'],
    67	
    68	    // Shorthand CSS Variables should be converted to the new syntax, even if
    69	    // the fallback contains functions. The fallback should also be migrated to
    70	    // the newest syntax.
    71	    ['bg-[--my-color,theme(colors.red.500)]', 'bg-(--my-color,var(--color-red-500))'],
    72	
    73	    // Both the positive and negative versions of arbitrary utilities should be
    74	    // converted to the bare value version.
    75	    ['mb-[32rem]', 'mb-128'],
    76	    ['mb-[-32rem]', '-mb-128'],

import { __unstable__loadDesignSystem } from '"'"'@tailwindcss/node'"'"'
import { migrateContents } from '"'"'./packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/migrate'"'"'
import { expect, vi } from '"'"'vitest'"'"'
import * as versions from '"'"'./packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/utils/version'"'"'

// Mock version to be major 3, so that migrations are active
vi.spyOn(versions, '"'"'isMajor'"'"').mockReturnValue(true)

async function run() {
  const designSystem = await __unstable__loadDesignSystem(
    `@import "tailwindcss";`,
    { base: process.cwd() }
  )

  const template = `
    <script>
      const flex = "grow"
      const shadow = "shadow"
      const onClick = (e) => {
        console.log(e)
      }
    </script>
    <div class="flex-grow shadow shadow-sm"></div>
  `

  const migrated = await migrateContents(designSystem, null, template, '"'"'svelte'"'"')
  console.log('"'"'--- Migrated Template ---'"'"')
  console.log(migrated)
  console.log('"'"'--------------------------'"'"')

  if (migrated.includes('"'"'const flex = "grow"'"'"')) {
      console.log('"'"'Reproduction success: content outside class names was migrated!'"'"')
  } else {
      console.log('"'"'Content outside class names was NOT migrated.'"'"')
  }
  
  if (migrated.includes('"'"'class="grow shadow-sm shadow-xs"'"'"')) {
      console.log('"'"'Class names were correctly migrated.'"'"')
  }
}

run().catch(console.error)
'

     1	import { __unstable__loadDesignSystem } from '@tailwindcss/node'
     2	import { expect, test, vi } from 'vitest'
     3	import * as versions from '../../utils/version'
     4	import { migrateCandidate } from './migrate'
     5	vi.spyOn(versions, 'isMajor').mockReturnValue(true)
     6	
     7	test('does not replace classes in invalid positions', async () => {
     8	  let designSystem = await __unstable__loadDesignSystem('@import "tailwindcss";', {
     9	    base: __dirname,
    10	  })
    11	
    12	  async function shouldNotReplace(example: string, candidate = '!border') {
    13	    expect(
    14	      await migrateCandidate(designSystem, {}, candidate, {
    15	        contents: example,
    16	        start: example.indexOf(candidate),
    17	        end: example.indexOf(candidate) + candidate.length,
    18	      }),
    19	    ).toEqual(candidate)
    20	  }
    21	
    22	  await shouldNotReplace(`let notBorder = !border    \n`)
    23	  await shouldNotReplace(`{ "foo": !border.something + ""}\n`)
    24	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-if="something && !border"></div>\n`)
    25	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-else-if="something && !border"></div>\n`)
    26	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-show="something && !border"></div>\n`)
    27	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-if="!border || !border"></div>\n`)
    28	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-else-if="!border || !border"></div>\n`)
    29	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-show="!border || !border"></div>\n`)
    30	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-if="!border"></div>\n`)
    31	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-else-if="!border"></div>\n`)
    32	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-show="!border"></div>\n`)
    33	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div x-if="!border"></div>\n`)
    34	
    35	  await shouldNotReplace(`let notShadow = shadow    \n`, 'shadow')
    36	  await shouldNotReplace(`{ "foo": shadow.something + ""}\n`, 'shadow')
    37	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-if="something && shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    38	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-else-if="something && shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    39	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-show="something && shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    40	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-if="shadow || shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    41	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-else-if="shadow || shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    42	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-show="shadow || shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    43	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-if="shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    44	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-else-if="shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    45	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div v-show="shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    46	  await shouldNotReplace(`<div x-if="shadow"></div>\n`, 'shadow')
    47	  await shouldNotReplace(
    48	    `<div style={{filter: 'drop-shadow(30px 10px 4px #4444dd)'}}/>\n`,

    50	  )
    51	
    52	  // Next.js Image placeholder cases
    53	  await shouldNotReplace(`<Image placeholder="blur" src="/image.jpg" />`, 'blur')
